<script>

    function saveSession(sport) 
    {
        $.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
		
    }

</script>

<script>
$(function() {
	$('body').addClass('collapsed');
	$('.nav-toggle').on('click', function() {
		if ($('#main-navigation').hasClass('expanded')) {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=collapsed; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		} else {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=expanded; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		}
	});
	$('.nav-comp-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-sports').hide();
		$('.nav-comps').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-comps').hide();
		$('.nav-sports').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport').on('click', function() {
		var sport = $(this).data('id');
		$.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
	});
	
	$('.nav-search input').on('input', function() {
		var val = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
		var items = $(this).parent().parent().find('.nav-item-wrapper > *');
		
		if (val != '') {
			items.hide();
			
			items.each(function(el) {
				if ($(this).text().toLowerCase().indexOf(val) >= 0) {
					$(this).show();
				}
			});
		} else {
			items.show();
		}
	});
});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
        $('#lock').click(function(){
            if($(this).prop("checked") == true){
				$('.lock').prop("checked",true);
            }
            else if($(this).prop("checked") == false){
				$('.lock').prop("checked",false);
            }
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$('#season_team').on('change', function() { 
	var val = $(this).val();
	if (val > 0) {
		location.href = 'people_edit_multiple.php?t=16378&season_id=' + this.value;
	}
	else {
		location.href = 'people_edit_multiple.php?t=16378';
	}

});
$('.year_went_pro').on('change', function() {
	var counter = 0;
	$('.year_went_pro').each(function() {
		
		var pro_value = $(this).val();
		if ((pro_value < 1900 || pro_value > 2100) && pro_value != '') {
			counter++;
			$(this).css('background-color', 'red');
		} else {
			$(this).css('background-color', 'white');
		}
		
		
	});
	if (counter == 0) {
		$('input[type=submit]').prop('disabled', false);
	} else {
		$('input[type=submit]').prop('disabled', true);
	}
	console.log(counter);
});
$(function() {
	$(".auto").autocomplete({
		source: "./internal/autosearch_city.php",
		minLength: 2
	});	

});
</script>
